==== Ilias 23 ====
(1) ὣς(Adv) οἳ(Pr)(N) μὲν(Pt) στενάχοντο(Imp)(M/P) κατὰ(Prp) πτόλιν(A)· αὐτὰρ(Kon) Ἀχαιοὶ(N)
(1) so sie aber seufzten hinab|durch Stadt· aber Achäer
(1) thus those indeed were|groaning throughout city· but Achaeans
(2) ἦ(Pt) ἐ(Pt) πεὶ(Kon) δὴ(Pt) νῆας(A) τε(Pt) καὶ(Kon) Ἑλλήσποντον(A) ἵκοντο(AorS)(M/P),
(2) ja dann als eben Schiffe auch und Hellespont kamen|sie,
(2) indeed then when now ships and and Hellespont came,

(3) sie aber nun zerstreuten|sich seine|eigene zu Schiff jeder,
(3) those indeed then were|scattering his|own upon ship each,

(4) Myrmidonen aber nicht ließ weg|zerstreuen Achilleus,
(4) Myrmidons but not allowed away scatter, Achilles

(5) but he indeed to the|companions war|loving spoke|among·

(6) Myrmidons swift|horsed to|me trusty companions

(7) not now yet from the|chariots let|us|loosen single|hoofed horses,

(8) but with the|horses and chariots nearer going

(9) Patroklos beweinen|wir· dies denn Ehrengabe ist der|Gestorbenen.
(9) Patroklos let|us|weep· this for privilege is of|the|having|died.

(10) but when indeed of|baneful shall|we|have|been|satisfied of|lament,

(12) thus he|spoke, those but wailed all|together, was|leading but Achilles.
